Facilities: The facilities are complete, there are relatively few fitness equipment, there are not many places for children to play, and the swimming pool is relatively small. There are more than 6 people in the room, so it seems very crowded!
Hygiene: Good hygiene, nothing to say, the toilet and bed are very clean! Environment: The environment is very good, right by the sea, there is also a reef bar to hang out, the room has a sea view, sitting on the balcony with the sea breeze and tea is very comfortable. Service: The service is good. The front desk knew that my wife's birthday was a special cake, and it was unexpectedly delicious!
Then let's talk about the disadvantages:
The management is not good. There are many tour groups on 61, and the individual tourists are not distinguished at all. The queue is half an hour, because there is a tour group in front of us who took dozens of ID cards to open the room, and there are few people at the front desk, and we waited until we were speechless! !It rained on 61 Typhoon, the ground was slippery, and the hotel did not wipe the water in time, causing a child to fall on the back of his head. msg:The environment, facilities and services are all very good and impeccable. It is considered the best and newest hotel in Huidong. The swimming pool is not open. It would be more fun if it was opened. The advantages of hardware and design are obvious, but I would like to make a suggestion. When the hotel receives group travelers, the meals should be separated from those of ordinary individual travelers. The reasons are: 1. Group travelers are very noisy, which makes the restaurant look like a canteen. The environment was originally good, but it has become very low. 2. Group travelers are mainly middle-aged and elderly. I witnessed with my own eyes that they used their own forks to directly fork the food on the plate and put it directly into their mouths at the buffet, and then used the same fork to directly fork the next plate of food, and so on. I was stunned at the time and stood and watched for a long time to see how the staff would deal with it. In the end, no one came to deal with it. Other guests were also stunned when they saw it, and then walked away silently. The staff may be afraid of trouble and pretend not to see it, but other guests immediately lost their appetite when they saw it. Of course, the elderly may not do it on purpose, and we are tolerant. The problem lies with the hotel staff. They did not provide timely guidance and prevention to change the food, which affected other guests. Therefore, I think that if you want to do group meals, you should separate it from individual guests.

üìçDetailed address: Huizhou Shuangyue Bay Sunrise Silver Sand Salt Crystal Hotel
üöóTraffic strategy:
Self-driving navigation Huizhou Shuangyue Bay Sunrise Silver Sand Salt Crystal Hotel. About 3 and a half hours from Guangzhou.

üåüHighlights and features
Comprehensive evaluation The beach and sea view are excellent, the reef bar is excellent for filming, and the balcony of the room is excellent for watching the sea. There is room for further improvement in the quality of hotel public services.
1. The exterior design of the hotel is cool, and the workmanship in the lobby is acceptable. The location of the hotel is quiet and the parking is convenient.
2. All hotel rooms face the sea, unlike the 369 advertised by the hotel, which differentiates various rooms. But it is practically recommended to live as high as possible, after all, the higher the view, the better.
3. It is better to take pictures of facilities such as seaside richu and heartbeat board.
4. There are free drinks such as Coca-Cola and Perrier in the refrigerator bar in the room, which is more considerate.
5. The lobby bar of the hotel is connected to the seaside beach, seaside hot spring and swimming pool. More convenient.
6. The room has a large viewing balcony. The balcony is equipped with high tables, chairs, and sofas. You can drink beer facing the sea, or lie down and watch the sea breeze.
7. The room is equipped with disposable towels and toilet mats. This should be praised.

‚úÖMust experience:
Fireworks can be set off at night on the beach, so you can prepare a little surprise for your companions

‚úÖMust experience:
The sunrise and sunset by the sea are beautiful. Although there are no beach chairs, you can walk along the beach and hold hands to welcome a sunset or sunrise.

‚úÖMust experience:
Hotel guests can enjoy unlimited visits to the Sunrise Reef Bar next to the hotel

‚úÖMust experience:
The rice roll shop, seafood or barbecue shop opened by the aborigines in the town where the hotel is located is relatively affordable. It is recommended to negotiate the price with the store after observing the experience.

msg:Summary: Generally speaking, this is a very good seaside tour. If the total score is 10 points, you can score 9 points. The hotel is still under construction, there must be many surprises, and I will come again.

advantage:
1. The room is completely in line with the picture display, the environment is very beautiful, you can see the boundless coast in the room.
2. The room is basically facing the sea. As a Cantonese who often travels by the sea, it is rare to have a seaside resort that makes people happy and unforgettable.
3. Rich entertainment facilities, there are different swimming pools for adults and children, and there are also waterways for boating. The boating fee is paid separately, 68 yuan per person. There is a bar in the hotel, and it is very comfortable to sit and relax with a cold drink, and it is very comfortable to lie down and blow the sea breeze. There will also be fireworks at night, although it is a small fireworks haha. Everyone's needs are different, I prefer to be relaxed and quiet.
4. Take housekeeper service, whether the front desk lobby customer service or the housekeeper customer service, the service is very good. The housekeepers Ada, Linn, and Eddy must be commended for not only upgrading the room, but also paying attention to the needs of the guests and helping to arrange pick-up and drop-off services from nearby restaurants.
5. The breakfast is so good. Compared with so many five-star hotels, I think this breakfast is really rich and has quality control.

shortcoming:
1. The room has a smell of decoration, maybe because it has just been decorated, it needs to be strengthened in deodorization.
2. The catering is not perfect, only breakfast buffet is currently available. The dinner is sold in the form of a set meal, and the price is not very cost-effective. Looking forward to the dinner buffet, it should be very good.
3. The driver of the battery car is very rude, and the service needs to be strengthened. It should not be a pain point for this resort. After all, the service attitude of other people is really good.

Suggest:
Most of the fabric sofas in the public seats of the lobby bar, pay attention to hygiene
